## Section 6: Recommended Batch Actions

1. Items to archive immediately: `4`
   Archive Category 1 rows first. They are the cleanest long-stale rows with no visible finance signal and no workshop-arrival signal.

2. Customer follow-up campaign list: `114`
   Suggested templates:
   - `Quote Sent`: 'We sent your quote on <date>. Let us know by <deadline> if you want to proceed, otherwise we will close the job.'
   - `Awaiting Confirmation / Booking Confirmed / Expecting Device`: 'Do you still want to proceed with this repair? If not, we will close the booking.'
   - `Repair Paused / Awaiting Part`: 'Your job is still open pending your confirmation/parts decision. Reply if you want us to keep it active.'

3. Finance review list (for Ricky/accountant): `350`
   Review every Category 3 row before cleanup. Priority order is the top of Section 4 because the table is sorted by visible value surface descending.

4. Leads to purge vs re-engage: purge `90`, re-engage `254`
   Use a single last-touch re-engagement on the positive subset, then purge/archive the rest from the active queue.

## Notes

- `Days since last status change` is taken from live `status4` activity logs where available; otherwise it falls back to the closest visible status-date field or item update timestamp.
- `Days stale` is based on the latest visible operational touch across updates, status movement, lifecycle dates, payment dates, and item update timestamps.
- Monday payment fields are known to be incomplete, so the finance exposure surface here is a review queue, not a final ledger.
